9-32 Decklists
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 26, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











There is more to this event than just the [Top 8](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gputr17/event-coverage/top-8-decklists-2017-02-26). Below are the decklists of the players who finished in 9th through 32nd place. Almost all of them were at most one match win and/or a tiebreaker boost away from the Top 8.
